 ) Union Telecom and Information Technology Minister Ravi Shankar Prasad has said that India is second only to China in terms of accessibility to the Internet among 300 million people

 Ravi Shankar Prasad was addressing the third Web Ratna Awards ceremony in Delhi on Wednesday
 unhone kaha ki is tarah bharat samaaj ko digital tareeke se badalane ke liye taiyaar he
 He said that the objective of Digital India program is to make the government comfortable and to bridge the gap between the rich and the poor in a digital way
 unhone bataaya ki sarkaar jald hi sarkari prashasan main paardarshita or saakh kii prakriya ko majboot banane ke liye open software niti laaegi
 Postal departments and Common Service Centers have been deployed to empower the underprivileged through digitization
 saamaanya seva kendron kii sankhya lagbhag chaar lakh hai
 The Web Ratna Awards are given in recognition of notable initiatives in the field of e-governance
 web ratna puraskaar ne apni anuthi pahal se vibhinn sarkari vibhaagon main gunvattta or maatra kii drushti se samgr vikaas main yogadan diya he
 The e-governance efforts of government ministries and departments are evaluated in various categories
 teen puraskaar- platinum, swarna va rajat, prayek shrenee main vijetaon ko die gaye
 The winners were selected on the basis of nominations received from each category
 naagarik kendrit seva shrenee main passport seva pariyojna ko platinum puraskaar mila
 The National Safai Karamcharis Finance Development Corporation and the National Open Schooling Institute received gold and silver awards respectively
 open data champion shrenee main register general tathaa janaganana ayukta karyaalay ko platinum puraskaar mila
 The Planning Commission and the Ministry of Statistics and Program Implementation received the Gold Award
 rajat puraskaar jal sansaadhan mantralay ko mila
 m Kisan - Government of India Portal received a platinum award for farmer-centric services in the innovative use of technology category
 swarna puraskaar madhya pradesh vaanijya kar vibhaag tathaa vaanijya kar vibhaag, tamilnadu ko mila

 utkrisht content shrenee main videsh mantralay ko platinum puraskaar mila
 The Ministry of Tribal Affairs, Kerala Tourism and the Ministry of Development of North Eastern Region received gold and silver awards respectively
